\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0060. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Calculate the derivative of the following function:

\input{Derivative-Compute-0060.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = {\frac{{\left(x + 10\right)} {\left(x + 7\right)}}{x^{2} - 49}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{2 \, {\left(x + 10\right)} {\left(x + 7\right)} x}{{\left(x^{2} - 49\right)}^{2}} + \frac{x + 10}{x^{2} - 49} + \frac{x + 7}{x^{2} - 49}}$
\end{problem}}


\latexProblemContent{

\end{problem}}

\end{problem}}

\end{problem}}

$f(x) = {\frac{{\left(x - 1\right)} {\left(x - 10\right)}}{x^{2} - 1}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{2 \, {\left(x - 1\right)} {\left(x - 10\right)} x}{{\left(x^{2} - 1\right)}^{2}} + \frac{x - 1}{x^{2} - 1} + \frac{x - 10}{x^{2} - 1}}$
\end{problem}}

\input{Derivative-Compute-0060.HELP.tex}

$f(x) = {\frac{{\left(x + 4\right)} {\left(x - 9\right)}}{x^{2} - 4}}$

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{2 \, {\left(x + 4\right)} {\left(x - 9\right)} x}{{\left(x^{2} - 4\right)}^{2}} + \frac{x + 4}{x^{2} - 4} + \frac{x - 9}{x^{2} - 4}}$
\end{problem}}

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{2 \, {\left(x - 4\right)} {\left(x - 8\right)} x}{{\left(x^{2} - 49\right)}^{2}} + \frac{x - 4}{x^{2} - 49} + \frac{x - 8}{x^{2} - 49}}$
\end{problem}}

$f'(x) = \answer{-\frac{2 \, {\left(x + 2\right)}^{2} x}{{\left(x^{2} - 49\right)}^{2}} + \frac{2 \, {\left(x + 2\right)}}{x^{2} - 49}}$
\end{problem}}
